        <td id="L191" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="191"></td>
        <td id="LC191" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When I do count the clock that tells the time,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L192" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="192"></td>
        <td id="LC192" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And see the brave day sunk in hideous night;</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L193" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="193"></td>
        <td id="LC193" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When I behold the violet past prime,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L194" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="194"></td>
        <td id="LC194" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And sable curls, all silvered o&#39;er with white;</td>

        <td id="L195" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="195"></td>
        <td id="LC195" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When lofty trees I see barren of leaves,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L196" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="196"></td>

        <td id="L197" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="197"></td>

        <td id="L200" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="200"></td>

        <td id="L211" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="211"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L212" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="212"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L213" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="213"></td>
        <td id="LC213" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Find no determination; then you were</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L214" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="214"></td>

        <td id="L215" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="215"></td>

      <tr>

        <td id="LC385" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  O&#39;ercharg&#39;d with burthen of mine own love&#39;s might.</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L386" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="386"></td>
        <td id="LC386" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  O! let my looks be then the eloquence</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L387" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="387"></td>
        <td id="LC387" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And dumb presagers of my speaking breast,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L388" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="388"></td>
        <td id="LC388" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Who plead for love, and look for recompense,</td>

        <td id="L389" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="389"></td>

        <td id="L390" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="390"></td>

        <td id="L391" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="391"></td>
        <td id="LC391" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    To hear with eyes belongs to love&#39;s fine wit.</td>

        <td id="LC396" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thy beauty&#39;s form in table of my heart;</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L397" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="397"></td>
        <td id="LC397" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  My body is the frame wherein &#39;tis held,</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L398" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="398"></td>
        <td id="LC398" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And perspective it is best painter&#39;s art.</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L399" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="399"></td>

        <td id="L400" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="400"></td>
        <td id="LC400" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To find where your true image pictur&#39;d lies,</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L401" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="401"></td>

        <td id="L402" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="402"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L403" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="403"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L404" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="404"></td>
        <td id="LC404" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Mine eyes have drawn thy shape, and thine for me</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L405" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="405"></td>

      <tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L412" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="412"></td>

        <td id="L416" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="416"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L482" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="482"></td>
        <td id="LC482" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And trouble deaf heaven with my bootless cries,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L483" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="483"></td>
        <td id="LC483" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And look upon myself, and curse my fate,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L484" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="484"></td>
        <td id="LC484" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Wishing me like to one more rich in hope,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L485" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="485"></td>
        <td id="LC485" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Featur&#39;d like him, like him with friends possess&#39;d,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L486" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="486"></td>
        <td id="LC486" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Desiring this man&#39;s art, and that man&#39;s scope,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L487" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="487"></td>
        <td id="LC487" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  With what I most enjoy contented least;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L488" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="488"></td>
        <td id="LC488" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Yet in these thoughts my self almost despising,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L489" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="489"></td>
        <td id="LC489" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Haply I think on thee,-- and then my state,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L490" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="490"></td>
        <td id="LC490" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Like to the lark at break of day arising</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L491" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="491"></td>
        <td id="LC491" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  From sullen earth, sings hymns at heaven&#39;s gate;</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L492" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="492"></td>
        <td id="LC492" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    For thy sweet love remember&#39;d such wealth brings</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L493" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="493"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L499" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="499"></td>

        <td id="L500" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="500"></td>

        <td id="L501" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="501"></td>

        <td id="L502" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="502"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L503" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="503"></td>
        <td id="LC503" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And weep afresh love&#39;s long since cancell&#39;d woe,</td>

        <td id="L504" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="504"></td>

        <td id="L506" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="506"></td>

        <td id="L518" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="518"></td>

        <td id="L520" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="520"></td>

        <td id="L522" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="522"></td>
        <td id="LC522" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thou art the grave where buried love doth live,</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L523" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="523"></td>
        <td id="LC523" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Hung with the trophies of my lovers gone,</td>

        <td id="LC577" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Ah! but those tears are pearl which thy love sheds,</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L578" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="578"></td>
        <td id="LC578" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    And they are rich and ransom all ill deeds.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L580" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="580"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L581" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="581"></td>
        <td id="LC581" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L582" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="582"></td>
        <td id="LC582" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  No more be griev&#39;d at that which thou hast done:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L583" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="583"></td>
        <td id="LC583" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Roses have thorns, and silver fountains mud:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L584" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="584"></td>
        <td id="LC584" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Clouds and eclipses stain both moon and sun,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L585" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="585"></td>
        <td id="LC585" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And loathsome canker lives in sweetest bud.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L586" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="586"></td>
        <td id="LC586" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  All men make faults, and even I in this,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L587" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="587"></td>
        <td id="LC587" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Authorizing thy trespass with compare,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L588" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="588"></td>
        <td id="LC588" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Myself corrupting, salving thy amiss,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L589" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="589"></td>
        <td id="LC589" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Excusing thy sins more than thy sins are;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L590" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="590"></td>
        <td id="LC590" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For to thy sensual fault I bring in sense,--</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L591" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="591"></td>
        <td id="LC591" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thy adverse party is thy advocate,--</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L592" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="592"></td>
        <td id="LC592" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And &#39;gainst myself a lawful plea commence:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L593" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="593"></td>
        <td id="LC593" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Such civil war is in my love and hate,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L594" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="594"></td>
        <td id="LC594" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    That I an accessary needs must be,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L595" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="595"></td>
        <td id="LC595" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    To that sweet thief which sourly robs from me.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L596" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="596"></td>
        <td id="LC596" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>

        <td id="LC597" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  XXXVI</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L598" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="598"></td>
        <td id="LC598" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L599" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="599"></td>
        <td id="LC599" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Let me confess that we two must be twain,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L600" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="600"></td>
        <td id="LC600" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Although our undivided loves are one:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L601" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="601"></td>
        <td id="LC601" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  So shall those blots that do with me remain,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L602" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="602"></td>
        <td id="LC602" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Without thy help, by me be borne alone.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L603" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="603"></td>
        <td id="LC603" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In our two loves there is but one respect,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L604" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="604"></td>
        <td id="LC604" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Though in our lives a separable spite,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L605" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="605"></td>
        <td id="LC605" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which though it alter not love&#39;s sole effect,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L606" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="606"></td>
        <td id="LC606" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Yet doth it steal sweet hours from love&#39;s delight.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L607" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="607"></td>
        <td id="LC607" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I may not evermore acknowledge thee,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L608" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="608"></td>
        <td id="LC608" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Lest my bewailed guilt should do thee shame,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L609" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="609"></td>
        <td id="LC609" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Nor thou with public kindness honour me,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L610" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="610"></td>
        <td id="LC610" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Unless thou take that honour from thy name:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L611" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="611"></td>
        <td id="LC611" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    But do not so, I love thee in such sort,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L612" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="612"></td>
        <td id="LC612" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    As thou being mine, mine is thy good report.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L616" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="616"></td>
        <td id="LC616" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  As a decrepit father takes delight</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L617" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="617"></td>
        <td id="LC617" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To see his active child do deeds of youth,</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L618" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="618"></td>
        <td id="LC618" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  So I, made lame by Fortune&#39;s dearest spite,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L619" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="619"></td>
        <td id="LC619" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Take all my comfort of thy worth and truth;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L620" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="620"></td>
        <td id="LC620" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For whether beauty, birth, or wealth, or wit,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L621" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="621"></td>
        <td id="LC621" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Or any of these all, or all, or more,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L622" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="622"></td>
        <td id="LC622" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Entitled in thy parts, do crowned sit,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L623" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="623"></td>
        <td id="LC623" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I make my love engrafted, to this store:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L624" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="624"></td>
        <td id="LC624" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  So then I am not lame, poor, nor despis&#39;d,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L625" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="625"></td>
        <td id="LC625" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Whilst that this shadow doth such substance give</td>

        <td id="L626" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="626"></td>
        <td id="LC626" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That I in thy abundance am suffic&#39;d,</td>

        <td id="L627" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="627"></td>

        <td id="LC629" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    This wish I have; then ten times happy me!</td>

        <td id="L633" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="633"></td>
        <td id="LC633" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  How can my muse want subject to invent,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L634" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="634"></td>
        <td id="LC634" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  While thou dost breathe, that pour&#39;st into my verse</td>

        <td id="L635" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="635"></td>
        <td id="LC635" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thine own sweet argument, too excellent</td>

        <td id="L636" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="636"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L637" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="637"></td>
        <td id="LC637" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  O! give thy self the thanks, if aught in me</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L638" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="638"></td>
        <td id="LC638" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Worthy perusal stand against thy sight;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L639" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="639"></td>
        <td id="LC639" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For who&#39;s so dumb that cannot write to thee,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L640" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="640"></td>
        <td id="LC640" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When thou thy self dost give invention light?</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L641" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="641"></td>
        <td id="LC641" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Be thou the tenth Muse, ten times more in worth</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L642" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="642"></td>
        <td id="LC642" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Than those old nine which rhymers invocate;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L643" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="643"></td>
        <td id="LC643" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And he that calls on thee, let him bring forth</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L644" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="644"></td>
        <td id="LC644" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Eternal numbers to outlive long date.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L645" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="645"></td>
        <td id="LC645" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    If my slight muse do please these curious days,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L646" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="646"></td>
        <td id="LC646" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    The pain be mine, but thine shall be the praise.</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L653" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="653"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L654" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="654"></td>
        <td id="LC654" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Even for this, let us divided live,</td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L657" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="657"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L658" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="658"></td>
        <td id="LC658" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  O absence! what a torment wouldst thou prove,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L659" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="659"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L660" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="660"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L661" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="661"></td>
        <td id="LC661" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which time and thoughts so sweetly doth deceive,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L662" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="662"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L663" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="663"></td>

        <td id="LC667" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Take all my loves, my love, yea take them all;</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L668" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="668"></td>
        <td id="LC668" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  What hast thou then more than thou hadst before?</td>

        <td id="L669" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="669"></td>
        <td id="LC669" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  No love, my love, that thou mayst true love call;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L670" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="670"></td>
        <td id="LC670" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  All mine was thine, before thou hadst this more.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L671" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="671"></td>
        <td id="LC671" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Then, if for my love, thou my love receivest,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L672" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="672"></td>
        <td id="LC672" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I cannot blame thee, for my love thou usest;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L673" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="673"></td>
        <td id="LC673" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But yet be blam&#39;d, if thou thy self deceivest</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L674" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="674"></td>
        <td id="LC674" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  By wilful taste of what thyself refusest.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L675" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="675"></td>
        <td id="LC675" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I do forgive thy robbery, gentle thief,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L676" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="676"></td>
        <td id="LC676" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Although thou steal thee all my poverty:</td>

      <tr>

        <td id="L1158" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1158"></td>
        <td id="LC1158" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  LXIX</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1159" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1159"></td>
        <td id="LC1159" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1160" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1160"></td>
        <td id="LC1160" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Those parts of thee that the world&#39;s eye doth view</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1161" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1161"></td>
        <td id="LC1161" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Want nothing that the thought of hearts can mend;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1162" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1162"></td>
        <td id="LC1162" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  All tongues--the voice of souls--give thee that due,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1163" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1163"></td>
        <td id="LC1163" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Uttering bare truth, even so as foes commend.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1164" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1164"></td>
        <td id="LC1164" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thy outward thus with outward praise is crown&#39;d;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1165" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1165"></td>
        <td id="LC1165" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But those same tongues, that give thee so thine own,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1166" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1166"></td>
        <td id="LC1166" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In other accents do this praise confound</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1167" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1167"></td>
        <td id="LC1167" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  By seeing farther than the eye hath shown.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1168" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1168"></td>
        <td id="LC1168" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  They look into the beauty of thy mind,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1169" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1169"></td>
        <td id="LC1169" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And that in guess they measure by thy deeds;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1170" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1170"></td>
        <td id="LC1170" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Then--churls--their thoughts, although their eyes were kind,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1171" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1171"></td>
        <td id="LC1171" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To thy fair flower add the rank smell of weeds:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1172" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1172"></td>
        <td id="LC1172" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    But why thy odour matcheth not thy show,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1173" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1173"></td>
        <td id="LC1173" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    The soil is this, that thou dost common grow.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1174" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1174"></td>
        <td id="LC1174" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1175" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1175"></td>
        <td id="LC1175" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  LXX</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1176" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1176"></td>
        <td id="LC1176" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1177" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1177"></td>
        <td id="LC1177" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That thou art blam&#39;d shall not be thy defect,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1178" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1178"></td>
        <td id="LC1178" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For slander&#39;s mark was ever yet the fair;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1179" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1179"></td>
        <td id="LC1179" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The ornament of beauty is suspect,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1180" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1180"></td>
        <td id="LC1180" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  A crow that flies in heaven&#39;s sweetest air.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1181" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1181"></td>
        <td id="LC1181" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  So thou be good, slander doth but approve</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1182" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1182"></td>
        <td id="LC1182" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thy worth the greater being woo&#39;d of time;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1183" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1183"></td>
        <td id="LC1183" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For canker vice the sweetest buds doth love,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1184" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1184"></td>
        <td id="LC1184" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And thou present&#39;st a pure unstained prime.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1185" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1185"></td>
        <td id="LC1185" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thou hast passed by the ambush of young days</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1186" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1186"></td>
        <td id="LC1186" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Either not assail&#39;d, or victor being charg&#39;d;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1187" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1187"></td>
        <td id="LC1187" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Yet this thy praise cannot be so thy praise,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1188" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1188"></td>
        <td id="LC1188" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To tie up envy, evermore enlarg&#39;d,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1189" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1189"></td>
        <td id="LC1189" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    If some suspect of ill mask&#39;d not thy show,</td>

        <td id="L1190" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1190"></td>
        <td id="LC1190" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Then thou alone kingdoms of hearts shouldst owe.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="L1194" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1194"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L1195" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1195"></td>
        <td id="LC1195" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Than you shall hear the surly sullen bell</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L1196" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1196"></td>
        <td id="LC1196" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Give warning to the world that I am fled</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1197" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1197"></td>
        <td id="LC1197" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  From this vile world with vilest worms to dwell:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1198" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1198"></td>
        <td id="LC1198" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Nay, if you read this line, remember not</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC1199" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The hand that writ it, for I love you so,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1200" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1200"></td>
        <td id="LC1200" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That I in your sweet thoughts would be forgot,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1201" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1201"></td>
        <td id="LC1201" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  If thinking on me then should make you woe.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1202" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1202"></td>
        <td id="LC1202" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  O! if,--I say you look upon this verse,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1203" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1203"></td>
        <td id="LC1203" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When I perhaps compounded am with clay,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1204" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1204"></td>
        <td id="LC1204" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Do not so much as my poor name rehearse;</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1205" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1205"></td>
        <td id="LC1205" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But let your love even with my life decay;</td>

      </tr>

        <td id="LC1213" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  After my death,--dear love, forget me quite,</td>

        <td id="L1214" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1214"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L1218" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1218"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L1219" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1219"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="LC1220" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That you for love speak well of me untrue,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1221" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1221"></td>
        <td id="LC1221" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  My name be buried where my body is,</td>

        <td id="L1224" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1224"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L1252" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1252"></td>
        <td id="LC1252" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  My spirit is thine, the better part of me:</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1253" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1253"></td>
        <td id="LC1253" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  So then thou hast but lost the dregs of life,</td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1255" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1255"></td>
        <td id="LC1255" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The coward conquest of a wretch&#39;s knife,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1256" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1256"></td>
        <td id="LC1256" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Too base of thee to be remembered.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1257" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1257"></td>
        <td id="LC1257" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    The worth of that is that which it contains,</td>

        <td id="LC1264" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And for the peace of you I hold such strife</td>

        <td id="L1284" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1284"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L1347" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1347"></td>
        <td id="LC1347" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  O! how I faint when I of you do write,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1348" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1348"></td>
        <td id="LC1348" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Knowing a better spirit doth use your name,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1349" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1349"></td>
        <td id="LC1349" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And in the praise thereof spends all his might,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1350" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1350"></td>
        <td id="LC1350" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To make me tongue-tied speaking of your fame!</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1351" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1351"></td>
        <td id="LC1351" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But since your worth--wide as the ocean is,--</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1352" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1352"></td>
        <td id="LC1352" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The humble as the proudest sail doth bear,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1353" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1353"></td>
        <td id="LC1353" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  My saucy bark, inferior far to his,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1354" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1354"></td>
        <td id="LC1354" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  On your broad main doth wilfully appear.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1355" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1355"></td>
        <td id="LC1355" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Your shallowest help will hold me up afloat,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1356" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1356"></td>
        <td id="LC1356" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Whilst he upon your soundless deep doth ride;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1357" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1357"></td>
        <td id="LC1357" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Or, being wrack&#39;d, I am a worthless boat,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1358" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1358"></td>
        <td id="LC1358" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  He of tall building, and of goodly pride:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1359" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1359"></td>
        <td id="LC1359" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Then if he thrive and I be cast away,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1360" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1360"></td>
        <td id="LC1360" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    The worst was this,--my love was my decay.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1361" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1361"></td>
        <td id="LC1361" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1362" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1362"></td>
        <td id="LC1362" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  LXXXI</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1363" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1363"></td>
        <td id="LC1363" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1364" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1364"></td>
        <td id="LC1364" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Or I shall live your epitaph to make,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1365" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1365"></td>
        <td id="LC1365" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Or you survive when I in earth am rotten;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1366" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1366"></td>
        <td id="LC1366" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  From hence your memory death cannot take,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1367" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1367"></td>
        <td id="LC1367" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Although in me each part will be forgotten.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1368" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1368"></td>
        <td id="LC1368" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Your name from hence immortal life shall have,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1369" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1369"></td>
        <td id="LC1369" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Though I, once gone, to all the world must die:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1370" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1370"></td>
        <td id="LC1370" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The earth can yield me but a common grave,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1371" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1371"></td>
        <td id="LC1371" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When you entombed in men&#39;s eyes shall lie.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1372" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1372"></td>
        <td id="LC1372" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Your monument shall be my gentle verse,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1373" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1373"></td>
        <td id="LC1373" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which eyes not yet created shall o&#39;er-read;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1374" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1374"></td>
        <td id="LC1374" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And tongues to be, your being shall rehearse,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1375" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1375"></td>
        <td id="LC1375" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When all the breathers of this world are dead;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1376" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1376"></td>
        <td id="LC1376" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    You still shall live,--such virtue hath my pen,--</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1377" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1377"></td>
        <td id="LC1377" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Where breath most breathes, even in the mouths of men.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1378" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1378"></td>
        <td id="LC1378" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1379" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1379"></td>
        <td id="LC1379" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  LXXXII</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1380" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1380"></td>
        <td id="LC1380" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1381" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1381"></td>
        <td id="LC1381" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I grant thou wert not married to my Muse,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1382" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1382"></td>
        <td id="LC1382" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And therefore mayst without attaint o&#39;erlook</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1383" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1383"></td>
        <td id="LC1383" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The dedicated words which writers use</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1384" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1384"></td>
        <td id="LC1384" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Of their fair subject, blessing every book.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1385" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1385"></td>
        <td id="LC1385" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thou art as fair in knowledge as in hue,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1386" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1386"></td>
        <td id="LC1386" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Finding thy worth a limit past my praise;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1387" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1387"></td>
        <td id="LC1387" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And therefore art enforced to seek anew</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1388" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1388"></td>
        <td id="LC1388" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Some fresher stamp of the time-bettering days.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1389" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1389"></td>
        <td id="LC1389" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And do so, love; yet when they have devis&#39;d,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1390" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1390"></td>
        <td id="LC1390" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  What strained touches rhetoric can lend,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1391" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1391"></td>
        <td id="LC1391" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thou truly fair, wert truly sympathiz&#39;d</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1392" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1392"></td>
        <td id="LC1392" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In true plain words, by thy true-telling friend;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1393" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1393"></td>
        <td id="LC1393" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    And their gross painting might be better us&#39;d</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1394" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1394"></td>
        <td id="LC1394" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Where cheeks need blood; in thee it is abus&#39;d.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1395" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1395"></td>
        <td id="LC1395" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1396" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1396"></td>
        <td id="LC1396" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  LXXXIII</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1397" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1397"></td>
        <td id="LC1397" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1398" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1398"></td>
        <td id="LC1398" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I never saw that you did painting need,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1399" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1399"></td>
        <td id="LC1399" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And therefore to your fair no painting set;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1400" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1400"></td>
        <td id="LC1400" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I found, or thought I found, you did exceed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1401" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1401"></td>
        <td id="LC1401" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That barren tender of a poet&#39;s debt:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1402" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1402"></td>
        <td id="LC1402" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And therefore have I slept in your report,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1403" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1403"></td>
        <td id="LC1403" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That you yourself, being extant, well might show</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1404" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1404"></td>
        <td id="LC1404" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  How far a modern quill doth come too short,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1405" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1405"></td>
        <td id="LC1405" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Speaking of worth, what worth in you doth grow.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1406" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1406"></td>
        <td id="LC1406" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  This silence for my sin you did impute,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1407" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1407"></td>
        <td id="LC1407" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which shall be most my glory being dumb;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1408" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1408"></td>
        <td id="LC1408" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For I impair not beauty being mute,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1409" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1409"></td>
        <td id="LC1409" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When others would give life, and bring a tomb.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1410" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1410"></td>
        <td id="LC1410" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    There lives more life in one of your fair eyes</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1411" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1411"></td>
        <td id="LC1411" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Than both your poets can in praise devise.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1412" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1412"></td>
        <td id="LC1412" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1413" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1413"></td>
        <td id="LC1413" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  LXXXIV</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1414" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1414"></td>
        <td id="LC1414" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1415" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1415"></td>
        <td id="LC1415" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Who is it that says most, which can say more,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1416" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1416"></td>
        <td id="LC1416" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Than this rich praise,--that you alone, are you?</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1417" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1417"></td>
        <td id="LC1417" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In whose confine immured is the store</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1418" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1418"></td>
        <td id="LC1418" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which should example where your equal grew.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1419" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1419"></td>
        <td id="LC1419" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Lean penury within that pen doth dwell</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1420" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1420"></td>
        <td id="LC1420" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That to his subject lends not some small glory;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1421" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1421"></td>
        <td id="LC1421" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But he that writes of you, if he can tell</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1422" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1422"></td>
        <td id="LC1422" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That you are you, so dignifies his story,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1423" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1423"></td>
        <td id="LC1423" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Let him but copy what in you is writ,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1424" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1424"></td>
        <td id="LC1424" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Not making worse what nature made so clear,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1425" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1425"></td>
        <td id="LC1425" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And such a counterpart shall fame his wit,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1426" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1426"></td>
        <td id="LC1426" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Making his style admired every where.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1427" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1427"></td>
        <td id="LC1427" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    You to your beauteous blessings add a curse,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1428" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1428"></td>
        <td id="LC1428" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Being fond on praise, which makes your praises worse.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1429" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1429"></td>
        <td id="LC1429" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1430" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1430"></td>
        <td id="LC1430" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  LXXXV</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1431" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1431"></td>
        <td id="LC1431" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1432" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1432"></td>
        <td id="LC1432" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  My tongue-tied Muse in manners holds her still,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1433" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1433"></td>
        <td id="LC1433" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  While comments of your praise richly compil&#39;d,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1434" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1434"></td>
        <td id="LC1434" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Reserve their character with golden quill,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1435" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1435"></td>
        <td id="LC1435" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And precious phrase by all the Muses fil&#39;d.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1436" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1436"></td>
        <td id="LC1436" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I think good thoughts, whilst others write good words,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1437" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1437"></td>
        <td id="LC1437" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And like unlettered clerk still cry &#39;Amen&#39;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1438" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1438"></td>
        <td id="LC1438" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To every hymn that able spirit affords,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1439" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1439"></td>
        <td id="LC1439" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In polish&#39;d form of well-refined pen.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1440" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1440"></td>
        <td id="LC1440" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Hearing you praised, I say &#39;&#39;tis so, &#39;tis true,&#39;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1441" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1441"></td>
        <td id="LC1441" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And to the most of praise add something more;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1442" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1442"></td>
        <td id="LC1442" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But that is in my thought, whose love to you,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1443" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1443"></td>
        <td id="LC1443" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Though words come hindmost, holds his rank before.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1444" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1444"></td>
        <td id="LC1444" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Then others, for the breath of words respect,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1445" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1445"></td>
        <td id="LC1445" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Me for my dumb thoughts, speaking in effect.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1446" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1446"></td>
        <td id="LC1446" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1448" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1448"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1449" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1449"></td>
        <td id="LC1449" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Was it the proud full sail of his great verse,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1450" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1450"></td>
        <td id="LC1450" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Bound for the prize of all too precious you,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1451" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1451"></td>
        <td id="LC1451" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That did my ripe thoughts in my brain inhearse,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1452" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1452"></td>
        <td id="LC1452" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Making their tomb the womb wherein they grew?</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1453" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1453"></td>
        <td id="LC1453" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Was it his spirit, by spirits taught to write,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1454" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1454"></td>
        <td id="LC1454" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Above a mortal pitch, that struck me dead?</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1455" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1455"></td>
        <td id="LC1455" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  No, neither he, nor his compeers by night</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1456" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1456"></td>
        <td id="LC1456" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Giving him aid, my verse astonished.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1457" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1457"></td>
        <td id="LC1457" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  He, nor that affable familiar ghost</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1458" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1458"></td>
        <td id="LC1458" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which nightly gulls him with intelligence,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1459" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1459"></td>
        <td id="LC1459" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  As victors of my silence cannot boast;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1460" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1460"></td>
        <td id="LC1460" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I was not sick of any fear from thence:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1461" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1461"></td>
        <td id="LC1461" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    But when your countenance fill&#39;d up his line,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1462" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1462"></td>
        <td id="LC1462" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Then lacked I matter; that enfeebled mine.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="L1466" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1466"></td>
        <td id="LC1466" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Farewell! thou art too dear for my possessing,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1467" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1467"></td>
        <td id="LC1467" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And like enough thou know&#39;st thy estimate,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1468" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1468"></td>
        <td id="LC1468" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The charter of thy worth gives thee releasing;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1469" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1469"></td>
        <td id="LC1469" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  My bonds in thee are all determinate.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1470" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1470"></td>
        <td id="LC1470" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For how do I hold thee but by thy granting?</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1471" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1471"></td>
        <td id="LC1471" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And for that riches where is my deserving?</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1472" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1472"></td>
        <td id="LC1472" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The cause of this fair gift in me is wanting,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1473" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1473"></td>
        <td id="LC1473" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And so my patent back again is swerving.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1474" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1474"></td>
        <td id="LC1474" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thy self thou gav&#39;st, thy own worth then not knowing,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1475" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1475"></td>
        <td id="LC1475" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Or me to whom thou gav&#39;st it, else mistaking;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1476" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1476"></td>
        <td id="LC1476" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  So thy great gift, upon misprision growing,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1477" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1477"></td>
        <td id="LC1477" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Comes home again, on better judgement making.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1478" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1478"></td>
        <td id="LC1478" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Thus have I had thee, as a dream doth flatter,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1479" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1479"></td>
        <td id="LC1479" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    In sleep a king, but waking no such matter.</td>

        <td id="L1484" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1484"></td>
        <td id="LC1484" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And place my merit in the eye of scorn,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1485" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1485"></td>
        <td id="LC1485" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Upon thy side, against myself I&#39;ll fight,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1486" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1486"></td>
        <td id="LC1486" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And prove thee virtuous, though thou art forsworn.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1487" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1487"></td>
        <td id="LC1487" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  With mine own weakness, being best acquainted,</td>

        <td id="L1488" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1488"></td>
        <td id="LC1488" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Upon thy part I can set down a story</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1489" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1489"></td>
        <td id="LC1489" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Of faults conceal&#39;d, wherein I am attainted;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1490" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1490"></td>
        <td id="LC1490" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That thou in losing me shalt win much glory:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1491" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1491"></td>
        <td id="LC1491" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And I by this will be a gainer too;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1492" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1492"></td>
        <td id="LC1492" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For bending all my loving thoughts on thee,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1493" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1493"></td>
        <td id="LC1493" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The injuries that to myself I do,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1494" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1494"></td>
        <td id="LC1494" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Doing thee vantage, double-vantage me.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1495" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1495"></td>
        <td id="LC1495" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Such is my love, to thee I so belong,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC1500" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Say that thou didst forsake me for some fault,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1501" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1501"></td>
        <td id="LC1501" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And I will comment upon that offence:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1502" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1502"></td>
        <td id="LC1502" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Speak of my lameness, and I straight will halt,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1503" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1503"></td>
        <td id="LC1503" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Against thy reasons making no defence.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1504" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1504"></td>
        <td id="LC1504" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thou canst not love disgrace me half so ill,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1505" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1505"></td>
        <td id="LC1505" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To set a form upon desired change,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1506" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1506"></td>
        <td id="LC1506" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  As I&#39;ll myself disgrace; knowing thy will,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1507" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1507"></td>
        <td id="LC1507" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I will acquaintance strangle, and look strange;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1508" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1508"></td>
        <td id="LC1508" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Be absent from thy walks; and in my tongue</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1509" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1509"></td>
        <td id="LC1509" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thy sweet beloved name no more shall dwell,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1510" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1510"></td>
        <td id="LC1510" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Lest I, too much profane, should do it wrong,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1511" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1511"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1512" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1512"></td>
        <td id="LC1512" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    For thee, against my self I&#39;ll vow debate,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1513" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1513"></td>
        <td id="LC1513" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    For I must ne&#39;er love him whom thou dost hate.</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L1520" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1520"></td>
        <td id="LC1520" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And do not drop in for an after-loss:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1521" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1521"></td>
        <td id="LC1521" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Ah! do not, when my heart hath &#39;scap&#39;d this sorrow,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1522" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1522"></td>
        <td id="LC1522" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Come in the rearward of a conquer&#39;d woe;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1523" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1523"></td>
        <td id="LC1523" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Give not a windy night a rainy morrow,</td>

        <td id="L1524" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1524"></td>
        <td id="LC1524" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To linger out a purpos&#39;d overthrow.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1525" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1525"></td>
        <td id="LC1525" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  If thou wilt leave me, do not leave me last,</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1526" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1526"></td>

        <td id="L1527" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1527"></td>
        <td id="LC1527" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But in the onset come: so shall I taste</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1528" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1528"></td>
        <td id="LC1528" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  At first the very worst of fortune&#39;s might;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1529" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1529"></td>
        <td id="LC1529" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    And other strains of woe, which now seem woe,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1530" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1530"></td>
        <td id="LC1530" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Compar&#39;d with loss of thee, will not seem so.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1531" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1531"></td>

        <td id="L1532" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1532"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1533" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1533"></td>
        <td id="LC1533" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1534" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1534"></td>
        <td id="LC1534" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Some glory in their birth, some in their skill,</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

        <td id="L1723" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1723"></td>
        <td id="LC1723" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I love not less, though less the show appear;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1724" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1724"></td>
        <td id="LC1724" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That love is merchandiz&#39;d, whose rich esteeming,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1725" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1725"></td>
        <td id="LC1725" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The owner&#39;s tongue doth publish every where.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1726" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1726"></td>
        <td id="LC1726" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Our love was new, and then but in the spring,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1727" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1727"></td>
        <td id="LC1727" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When I was wont to greet it with my lays;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1728" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1728"></td>
        <td id="LC1728" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  As Philomel in summer&#39;s front doth sing,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1729" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1729"></td>
        <td id="LC1729" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And stops her pipe in growth of riper days:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1730" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1730"></td>
        <td id="LC1730" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Not that the summer is less pleasant now</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1731" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1731"></td>
        <td id="LC1731" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Than when her mournful hymns did hush the night,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1732" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1732"></td>
        <td id="LC1732" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But that wild music burthens every bough,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1733" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1733"></td>
        <td id="LC1733" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And sweets grown common lose their dear delight.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1734" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1734"></td>
        <td id="LC1734" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Therefore like her, I sometime hold my tongue:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1735" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1735"></td>
        <td id="LC1735" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Because I would not dull you with my song.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1736" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1736"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1738" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1738"></td>
