        <td id="L1739" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1739"></td>
        <td id="LC1739" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Alack! what poverty my Muse brings forth,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1740" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1740"></td>
        <td id="LC1740" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That having such a scope to show her pride,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1741" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1741"></td>
        <td id="LC1741" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The argument, all bare, is of more worth</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1742" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1742"></td>
        <td id="LC1742" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Than when it hath my added praise beside!</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1743" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1743"></td>
        <td id="LC1743" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  O! blame me not, if I no more can write!</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1744" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1744"></td>
        <td id="LC1744" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Look in your glass, and there appears a face</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1745" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1745"></td>
        <td id="LC1745" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  That over-goes my blunt invention quite,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1746" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1746"></td>
        <td id="LC1746" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Dulling my lines, and doing me disgrace.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1747" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1747"></td>
        <td id="LC1747" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Were it not sinful then, striving to mend,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1748" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1748"></td>
        <td id="LC1748" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To mar the subject that before was well?</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1749" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1749"></td>
        <td id="LC1749" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For to no other pass my verses tend</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1750" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1750"></td>
        <td id="LC1750" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Than of your graces and your gifts to tell;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1751" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1751"></td>
        <td id="LC1751" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    And more, much more, than in my verse can sit,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1752" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1752"></td>
        <td id="LC1752" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Your own glass shows you when you look in it.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1755" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1755"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1756" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1756"></td>
        <td id="LC1756" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  To me, fair friend, you never can be old,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1757" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1757"></td>
        <td id="LC1757" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For as you were when first your eye I ey&#39;d,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1758" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1758"></td>
        <td id="LC1758" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Such seems your beauty still. Three winters cold,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1759" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1759"></td>
        <td id="LC1759" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Have from the forests shook three summers&#39; pride,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1760" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1760"></td>
        <td id="LC1760" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Three beauteous springs to yellow autumn turn&#39;d,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1761" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1761"></td>
        <td id="LC1761" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In process of the seasons have I seen,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1762" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1762"></td>
        <td id="LC1762" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Three April perfumes in three hot Junes burn&#39;d,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1763" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1763"></td>
        <td id="LC1763" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Since first I saw you fresh, which yet are green.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1764" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1764"></td>
        <td id="LC1764" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Ah! yet doth beauty like a dial-hand,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1765" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1765"></td>
        <td id="LC1765" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Steal from his figure, and no pace perceiv&#39;d;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1766" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1766"></td>
        <td id="LC1766" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  So your sweet hue, which methinks still doth stand,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1767" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1767"></td>
        <td id="LC1767" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Hath motion, and mine eye may be deceiv&#39;d:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L1768" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1768"></td>
        <td id="LC1768" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    For fear of which, hear this thou age unbred:</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC1774" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Nor my beloved as an idol show,</td>

        <td id="LC1778" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Still constant in a wondrous excellence;</td>

        <td id="L1779" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1779"></td>

        <td id="LC1780" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  One thing expressing, leaves out difference.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1781" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1781"></td>

        <td id="LC1782" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  &#39;Fair, kind, and true,&#39; varying to other words;</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1783" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1783"></td>

        <td id="L1812" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1812"></td>

        <td id="L1813" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1813"></td>

        <td id="L1815" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1815"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L1816" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1816"></td>
        <td id="LC1816" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  My love looks fresh, and Death to me subscribes,</td>

        <td id="L2197" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2197"></td>
        <td id="LC2197" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Coral is far more red, than her lips red:</td>

        <td id="L2202" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2202"></td>

        <td id="LC2573" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In act thy bed-vow broke, and new faith torn,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2574" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2574"></td>
        <td id="LC2574" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In vowing new hate after new love bearing:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2575" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2575"></td>
        <td id="LC2575" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But why of two oaths&#39; breach do I accuse thee,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2576" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2576"></td>
        <td id="LC2576" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  When I break twenty? I am perjur&#39;d most;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2577" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2577"></td>
        <td id="LC2577" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For all my vows are oaths but to misuse thee,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2578" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2578"></td>
        <td id="LC2578" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And all my honest faith in thee is lost:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2579" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2579"></td>
        <td id="LC2579" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For I have sworn deep oaths of thy deep kindness,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2580" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2580"></td>
        <td id="LC2580" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Oaths of thy love, thy truth, thy constancy;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2581" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2581"></td>
        <td id="LC2581" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And, to enlighten thee, gave eyes to blindness,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2582" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2582"></td>
        <td id="LC2582" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Or made them swear against the thing they see;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2583" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2583"></td>
        <td id="LC2583" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    For I have sworn thee fair; more perjur&#39;d I,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2584" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2584"></td>
        <td id="LC2584" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    To swear against the truth so foul a lie!</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2585" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2585"></td>
        <td id="LC2585" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2586" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2586"></td>
        <td id="LC2586" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  CLIII</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2587" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2587"></td>
        <td id="LC2587" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2588" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2588"></td>
        <td id="LC2588" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Cupid laid by his brand and fell asleep:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2589" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2589"></td>
        <td id="LC2589" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  A maid of Dian&#39;s this advantage found,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2590" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2590"></td>
        <td id="LC2590" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And his love-kindling fire did quickly steep</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2591" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2591"></td>
        <td id="LC2591" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  In a cold valley-fountain of that ground;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2592" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2592"></td>
        <td id="LC2592" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which borrow&#39;d from this holy fire of Love,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2593" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2593"></td>
        <td id="LC2593" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  A dateless lively heat, still to endure,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2594" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2594"></td>
        <td id="LC2594" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And grew a seeting bath, which yet men prove</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2595" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2595"></td>
        <td id="LC2595" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Against strange maladies a sovereign cure.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2596" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2596"></td>
        <td id="LC2596" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  But at my mistress&#39; eye Love&#39;s brand new-fired,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2597" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2597"></td>
        <td id="LC2597" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The boy for trial needs would touch my breast;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2598" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2598"></td>
        <td id="LC2598" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  I, sick withal, the help of bath desired,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2599" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2599"></td>
        <td id="LC2599" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And thither hied, a sad distemper&#39;d guest,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2600" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2600"></td>
        <td id="LC2600" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    But found no cure, the bath for my help lies</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2601" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2601"></td>
        <td id="LC2601" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Where Cupid got new fire; my mistress&#39; eyes.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2602" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2602"></td>
        <td id="LC2602" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2603" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2603"></td>
        <td id="LC2603" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  CLIV</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2604" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2604"></td>
        <td id="LC2604" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2605" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2605"></td>
        <td id="LC2605" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The little Love-god lying once asleep,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2606" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2606"></td>
        <td id="LC2606" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Laid by his side his heart-inflaming brand,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2607" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2607"></td>
        <td id="LC2607" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Whilst many nymphs that vow&#39;d chaste life to keep</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2608" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2608"></td>
        <td id="LC2608" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Came tripping by; but in her maiden hand</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2609" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2609"></td>
        <td id="LC2609" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  The fairest votary took up that fire</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2610" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2610"></td>
        <td id="LC2610" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which many legions of true hearts had warm&#39;d;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2611" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2611"></td>
        <td id="LC2611" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  And so the general of hot desire</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2612" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2612"></td>
        <td id="LC2612" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Was, sleeping, by a virgin hand disarm&#39;d.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2613" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2613"></td>
        <td id="LC2613" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  This brand she quenched in a cool well by,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2614" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2614"></td>
        <td id="LC2614" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Which from Love&#39;s fire took heat perpetual,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2615" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2615"></td>
        <td id="LC2615" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Growing a bath and healthful remedy,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2616" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2616"></td>
        <td id="LC2616" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  For men diseas&#39;d; but I, my mistress&#39; thrall,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2617" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2617"></td>
        <td id="LC2617" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Came there for cure and this by that I prove,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L2618" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="2618"></td>
        <td id="LC2618" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Love&#39;s fire heats water, water cools not love.</td>
      </tr>
